* as React from "react"
import * as DialogPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-dialog"
import { X } from "lucide-react"

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

const Dialog = DialogPrimitive.Root

const DialogTrigger = DialogPrimitive.Trigger

const DialogPortal = DialogPrimitive.Portal

const DialogClose = DialogPrimitive.Close

const DialogOverlay = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>
>(({ className, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPrimitive.Overlay
    ref={ref}
    className=
```

## License: unknown
https://github.com/zarybnicky/Sirimbo/blob/7b65f6d91d509ad4d70b285060ef513964991a18/%40app/ui/dialog.tsx

```
* as React from "react"
import * as DialogPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-dialog"
import { X } from "lucide-react"

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

const Dialog = DialogPrimitive.Root

const DialogTrigger = DialogPrimitive.Trigger

const DialogPortal = DialogPrimitive.Portal

const DialogClose = DialogPrimitive.Close

const DialogOverlay = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>
>(({ className, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPrimitive.Overlay
    ref={ref}
    className={cn(
      "fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/80 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data
```

## License: unknown
https://github.com/zarybnicky/Sirimbo/blob/7b65f6d91d509ad4d70b285060ef513964991a18/%40app/ui/dialog.tsx

```
* as React from "react"
import * as DialogPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-dialog"
import { X } from "lucide-react"

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

const Dialog = DialogPrimitive.Root

const DialogTrigger = DialogPrimitive.Trigger

const DialogPortal = DialogPrimitive.Portal

const DialogClose = DialogPrimitive.Close

const DialogOverlay = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>
>(({ className, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPrimitive.Overlay
    ref={ref}
    className={cn(
      "fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/80 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
))
DialogOverlay.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Overlay.
```


## License: Apache-2.0
https://github.com/theatre-js/theatre/blob/ec4ad14839265b40565ec76e22f736cecaee2be1/packages/app/src/ui/components/ui/dialog.tsx

```
* as React from "react"
import * as DialogPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-dialog"
import { X } from "lucide-react"

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

const Dialog = DialogPrimitive.Root

const DialogTrigger = DialogPrimitive.Trigger

const DialogPortal = DialogPrimitive.Portal

const DialogClose = DialogPrimitive.Close

const DialogOverlay = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>
>(({ className, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPrimitive.Overlay
    ref={ref}
    className={cn(
      "fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/80 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
))
DialogOverlay.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Overlay.
```

    ref={ref}
    className={cn(
      "fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/80 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
))
DialogOverlay.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Overlay.displayName

const DialogContent = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef
```

    {...props}
  />
))

  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>
>(({ className, children, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPortal>
    <DialogOverlay />
    <DialogPrimitive.Content
      ref={ref}
      className={cn(
        "fixed left-[50%] top-[50%] z-50 grid w-full max-w-lg translate-x-[-50%] translate-y-[-50%] gap-4 border bg

  <DialogPrimitive.Overlay
    ref={ref}
    className={cn(
      "fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/80 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
))
DialogOverlay.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Overlay.displayName

const DialogContent = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>
>(({ className, children, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPortal>
    <DialogOverlay />
    <DialogPrimitive.Content
      ref={ref}
      className={cn(
        "fixed left-[50%] top-[50%] z-50 grid w-full max-w-lg translate-x-[-50%] translate-y-[-50%] gap-4 border bg-background p-6 shadow-lg duration-200 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open
```

  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>

      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
))

* as React from "react"
import * as DialogPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-dialog"
import { X } from "lucide-react"

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

const Dialog = DialogPrimitive.Root

const DialogTrigger = DialogPrimitive.Trigger

const DialogPortal = DialogPrimitive.Portal

const DialogClose = DialogPrimitive.Close

const DialogOverlay = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>
>(({ className, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPrimitive.Overlay
    ref={ref}
    className={cn(
      "fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/80 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
))
DialogOverlay.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Overlay.displayName

const DialogContent = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>
>(({ className, children, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPortal>
    <DialogOverlay />
    <DialogPrimitive.Content
      ref={ref}
      className={cn(
        "fixed left-[50%] top-[50%] z-50 grid w-full max-w-lg translate-x-[-50%] translate-y-[-50%] gap-4 border bg-background p-6 shadow-lg duration-200 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0 data-[state=closed]:zoom-out-95 data-[state=open]:zoom-in-95 data-[state=closed]:slide
```

>(({ className, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPrimitive.Overlay
    ref={ref}
    className={cn(
      "fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/80 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
))
DialogOverlay.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Overlay.displayName

  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>
>(({ className, children, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPortal>
    <DialogOverlay />
    <DialogPrimitive.Content
      ref={ref}
      className={cn(

const DialogOverlay = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>
>(({ className, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPrimitive.Overlay
    ref={ref}
    className={cn(
      "fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/80 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
))
DialogOverlay.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Overlay.displayName

const DialogContent = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>
>(({ className, children, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPortal>
    <DialogOverlay />
    <DialogPrimitive.Content
      ref={ref}
      className={cn(
        "fixed left-[50%] top-[50%] z-50 grid w-full max-w-lg translate-x-[-50%] translate-y-[-50%] gap-4 border bg-background p-6 shadow-lg duration-200 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0 data-[state=closed]:zoom-out-95 data-[state=open]:zoom-in-95 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-left-1/2 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-top-[48%] data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-left-1/2 data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-top-[48%] sm:rounded-lg",
        className
      )}
      {...props}
    >
      {children}
      <DialogPrimitive.Close className="absolute right-4 top-4 rounded-sm opacity-70 ring-offset-background transition-opacity hover:opacity-100 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring focus:ring-offset-2 disabled:pointer-events-none data

import * as DialogPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-dialog"
import { X } from "lucide-react"

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

const Dialog = DialogPrimitive.Root

const DialogTrigger = DialogPrimitive.Trigger

const DialogPortal = DialogPrimitive.Portal

const DialogClose = DialogPrimitive.Close

const DialogOverlay = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>
>(({ className, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPrimitive.Overlay
    ref={ref}
    className={cn(
      "fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/80 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
))
DialogOverlay.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Overlay.displayName

const DialogContent = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>
>(({ className, children, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPortal>
    <DialogOverlay />
    <DialogPrimitive.Content
      ref={ref}
      className={cn(
        "fixed left-[50%] top-[50%] z-50 grid w-full max-w-lg translate-x-[-50%] translate-y-[-50%] gap-4 border bg-background p-6 shadow-lg duration-200 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0 data-[state=closed]:zoom-out-95 data-[state=open]:zoom-in-95 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-left-1/2 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-top-[48%] data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-left-1/2 data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-top-[48%] sm:rounded-lg",
        className
      )}
      {...props}
    >
      {children}
      <DialogPrimitive.Close className="absolute right-4 top-4 rounded-sm opacity-70 ring-offset-background transition-opacity hover
```

        "fixed left-[50%] top-[50%] z-50 grid w-full max-w-lg translate-x-[-50%] translate-y-[-50%] gap-4 border bg-background p-6 shadow-lg duration-200 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0 data-[state=closed]:zoom-out-95 data-[state=open]:zoom-in-95 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-left-1/2 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-top-[48%] data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-left-1/2 data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-top-[48%] sm:rounded-lg",
        className
      )}
      {...props}
    >
      {children}
      <DialogPrimitive.Close className="absolute right-4 top-4 rounded-sm opacity-70 ring-offset-background transition-opacity hover:opacity-100 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring focus:ring-offset-2 disabled:pointer-events-none data-[state=open]:bg-accent data-[state=open]:text-muted-foreground">
        <X className="h-4 w-4" />
        <span className="sr-only">Close</span>
      </DialogPrimitive.Close>
    </

  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>

  <DialogPortal>
    <DialogOverlay />
    <DialogPrimitive.Content
      ref={ref}
      className={cn(
        "fixed left-[50%] top-[50%] z-50 grid w-full max-w-lg translate-x-[-50%] translate-y-[-50%] gap-4 border bg-background p-6 shadow-lg duration-200 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0 data-[state=closed]:zoom-out-95 data-[state=open]:zoom-in-95 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-left-1/2 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-top-[48%] data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-left-1/2 data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-top-[48%] sm:rounded-lg",
        className
      )}
      {...props}
    >
      {children}
      <DialogPrimitive.Close className="absolute right-4 top-4 rounded-sm opacity-70 ring-offset-background transition-opacity hover:opacity-100 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring focus:ring-offset-2 disabled:pointer-events-none data-[state=open]:bg-accent data-[state=open]:text-muted-foreground">
        <X className="h-4 w-4" />
        <span className="sr-only">Close</span>
      </DialogPrimitive.Close>
    </DialogPrimitive.Content>
  </DialogPortal>
))
DialogContent.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Content
```

https://github.com/lacymorrow/cinematic/blob/174f07514c07898fe455f9fc1d3af0b992cb0015/src/components/ui/dialog.tsx

```
* as React from "react"
import * as DialogPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-dialog"
import { X } from "lucide-react"

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

const Dialog = DialogPrimitive.Root

const DialogTrigger = DialogPrimitive.Trigger

const DialogPortal = DialogPrimitive.Portal

const DialogClose = DialogPrimitive.Close

const DialogOverlay = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>
>(({ className, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPrimitive.Overlay
    ref={ref}
    className={cn(
      "fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/80 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
))
DialogOverlay.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Overlay.displayName

const DialogContent = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>
>(({ className, children, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPortal>
    <DialogOverlay />
    <DialogPrimitive.Content
      ref={ref}
      className={cn(
        "fixed left-[50%] top-[50%] z-50 grid w-full max-w-lg translate-x-[-50%] translate-y-[-50%] gap-4 border bg-background p-6 shadow-lg duration-200 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0 data-[state=closed]:zoom-out-95 data-[state=open]:zoom-in-95 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-left-1/2 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-top-[48%] data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-left-1/2 data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-top-[48%] sm:rounded-lg",
        className
      )}
      {...props}
    >
      {children}
      <DialogPrimitive.Close className="absolute right-4 top-4 rounded-sm opacity-70 ring-offset-background transition-opacity hover:opacity-100 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring focus:ring-offset-2 disabled:pointer-events-none data-[state=open]:bg-accent data-[state=open]:text-muted-foreground">
        <X className="h-4 w-4" />
        <span className="sr-only">
```

* as React from "react"
import * as DialogPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-dialog"
import { X } from "lucide-react"

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

const Dialog = DialogPrimitive.Root

const DialogTrigger = DialogPrimitive.Trigger

const DialogPortal = DialogPrimitive.Portal

const DialogClose = DialogPrimitive.Close

const DialogOverlay = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>
>(({ className, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPrimitive.Overlay
    ref={ref}
    className={cn(
      "fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/80 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
))
DialogOverlay.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Overlay.displayName

const DialogContent = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>
>(({ className, children, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPortal>
    <DialogOverlay />
    <DialogPrimitive.Content
      ref={ref}
      className={cn(
        "fixed left-[50%] top-[50%] z-50 grid w-full max-w-lg translate-x-[-50%] translate-y-[-50%] gap-4 border bg-background p-6 shadow-lg duration-200 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0 data-[state=closed]:zoom-out-95 data-[state=open]:zoom-in-95 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-left-1/2 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-top-[48%] data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-left-1/2 data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-top-[48%] sm:rounded-lg",
        className
      )}
      {...props}
    >
      {children}
      <DialogPrimitive.Close className="absolute right-4 top-4 rounded-sm opacity-70 ring-offset-background transition-opacity hover:opacity-100 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring focus:ring-offset-2 disabled:pointer-events-none data-[state=open]:bg-accent data-[state=open]:text-muted-foreground">
        <X className="h-4 w-4" />
        <span className="sr-only">
```

* as React from "react"
import * as DialogPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-dialog"
import { X } from "lucide-react"

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

const Dialog = DialogPrimitive.Root

const DialogTrigger = DialogPrimitive.Trigger

const DialogPortal = DialogPrimitive.Portal

const DialogClose = DialogPrimitive.Close

  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>
>(({ className, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPrimitive.Overlay
    ref={ref}
    className={cn(
      "fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/80 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
))
DialogOverlay.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Overlay.displayName

  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>
>(({ className, children, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPortal>
    <DialogOverlay />
    <DialogPrimitive.Content
      ref={ref}
      className={cn(
        "fixed left-[50%] top-[50%] z-50 grid w-full max-w-lg translate-x-[-50%] translate-y-[-50%] gap-4 border bg-background p-6 shadow-lg duration-200 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0 data-[state=closed]:zoom-out-95 data-[state=open]:zoom-in-95 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-left-1/2 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-top-[48%] data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-left-1/2 data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-top-[48%] sm:rounded-lg",
        className
      )}

* as React from "react"
import * as DialogPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-dialog"
import { X } from "lucide-react"

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

const Dialog = DialogPrimitive.Root

const DialogTrigger = DialogPrimitive.Trigger

const DialogPortal = DialogPrimitive.Portal

const DialogClose = DialogPrimitive.Close

const DialogOverlay = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>
>(({ className, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPrimitive.Overlay
    ref={ref}
    className={cn(
      "fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/80 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
))
DialogOverlay.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Overlay.displayName

const DialogContent = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>
>(({ className, children, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPortal>
    <DialogOverlay />
    <DialogPrimitive.Content
      ref={ref}
      className={cn(
        "fixed left-[50%] top-[50%] z-50 grid w-full max-w-lg translate-x-[-50%] translate-y-[-50%] gap-4 border bg-background p-6 shadow-lg duration-200 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0 data-[state=closed]:zoom-out-95 data-[state=open]:zoom-in-95 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-left-1/2 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-top-[48%] data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-left-1/2 data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-top-[48%] sm:rounded-lg",
        className
      )}
      {...props}
    >
      {children}
      <DialogPrimitive.Close className="absolute right-4 top-4 rounded-sm opacity-70 ring-offset-background transition-opacity hover:opacity-100 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring focus:ring-offset-2 disabled:pointer-events-none data-[state=open]:bg-accent data-[state=open]:text-muted-foreground">
        <X className="h-4 w-4" />
        <span className="sr-only">

  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>

  <DialogPrimitive.Overlay
    ref={ref}
    className={cn(
      "fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/80 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
))
DialogOverlay.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Overlay.displayName

  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>
>(({ className, children, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPortal>
    <DialogOverlay />
    <DialogPrimitive.Content
      ref={ref}
      className={cn(
        "fixed left-[50%] top-[50%] z-50 grid w-full max-w-lg translate-x-[-50%] translate-y-[-50%] gap-4 border bg-background p-6 shadow-lg duration-200 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0 data-[state=closed]:zoom-out-95 data-[state=open]:zoom-in-95 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-left-1/2 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-top-[48%] data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-left-1/2 data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-top-[48%] sm:rounded-lg",
        className
      )}
      {...props}
    >
      {children}
      <DialogPrimitive.Close className="absolute right-4 top-4 rounded-sm opacity-70 ring-offset-background transition-opacity hover:opacity-100 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring focus:ring-offset-2 disabled:pointer-events-none data-[state=open]:bg-accent data-[state=open]:text-muted-foreground">

        "fixed left-[50%] top-[50%] z-50 grid w-full max-w-lg translate-x-[-50%] translate-y-[-50%] gap-4 border bg-background p-6 shadow-lg duration-200 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0 data-[state=closed]:zoom-out-95 data-[state=open]:zoom-in-95 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-left-1/2 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-top-[48%] data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-left-1/2 data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-top-[48%] sm:rounded-lg",
        className
      )}
      {...props}
    >
      {children}
      <DialogPrimitive.Close className="absolute right-4 top-4 rounded-sm opacity-70 ring-offset-background transition-opacity hover:opacity-100 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring focus:ring-offset-2 disabled:pointer-events-none data-[state=open]:bg-accent data-[state=open]:text-muted-foreground">
        <X className="h-4 w-4" />

    <DialogOverlay />

        className
      )}
      {...props}
    >
      {children}
      <DialogPrimitive.Close className="absolute right-4 top-4 rounded-sm opacity-70 ring-offset-background transition-opacity hover:opacity-100 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring focus:ring-offset-2 disabled:pointer-events-none data-[state=open]:bg-accent data-[state=open]:text-muted-foreground">
        <X className="h-4 w-4" />
        <span className="sr-only">Close</span>
      </DialogPrimitive.Close>
    </DialogPrimitive.Content>
  </DialogPortal>

      <DialogPrimitive.Close className="absolute right-4 top-4 rounded-sm opacity-70 ring-offset-background transition-opacity hover:opacity-100 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring focus:ring-offset-2 disabled:pointer-events-none data-[state=open]:bg-accent data-[state=open]:text-muted-foreground">
        <X className="h-4 w-4" />
        <span className="sr-only">Close</span>
      </DialogPrimitive.Close>
    </DialogPrimitive.Content>
  </DialogPortal>
))
DialogContent.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Content.displayName

const DialogHeader = ({
  className,
  ...props
}: React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement>) => (
  <div
    className={cn(
      "flex flex-col space-y-1.5 text-center sm:text-left",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
)
DialogHeader.displayName = "DialogHeader"

const DialogFooter = ({
  className,
  ...props
}: React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement>) => (
  <div
    className={cn(
      "flex flex-col-reverse sm:flex-row sm:justify-end sm:space-x-2",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
)

>(({ className, children, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPortal>
    <DialogOverlay />
    <DialogPrimitive.Content
      ref={ref}
      className={cn(
        "fixed left-[50%] top-[50%] z-50 grid w-full max-w-lg translate-x-[-50%] translate-y-[-50%] gap-4 border bg-background p-6 shadow-lg duration-200 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0 data-[state=closed]:zoom-out-95 data-[state=open]:zoom-in-95 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-left-1/2 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-top-[48%] data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-left-1/2 data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-top-[48%] sm:rounded-lg",
        className
      )}
      {...props}
    >
      {children}
      <DialogPrimitive.Close className="absolute right-4 top-4 rounded-sm opacity-70 ring-offset-background transition-opacity hover:opacity-100 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring focus:ring-offset-2 disabled:pointer-events-none data-[state=open]:bg-accent data-[state=open]:text-muted-foreground">
        <X className="h-4 w-4" />
        <span className="sr-only">Close</span>
      </DialogPrimitive.Close>
    </DialogPrimitive.Content>
  </DialogPortal>
))
DialogContent.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Content.displayName

const DialogHeader = ({
  className,
  ...props
}: React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement>) => (
  <div
    className={cn(
      "flex flex-col space-y-1.5 text-center sm:text-left",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
)
DialogHeader.displayName = "DialogHeader"

const DialogFooter = ({
  className,
  ...props

  <div
    className={cn(
      "flex flex-col-reverse sm:flex-row sm:justify-end sm:space-x-2",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
)

  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.

  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>

    )}
    {...props}

  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>

        className
      )}
      {...props}
    >
      {children}
      <DialogPrimitive.Close className="absolute right-4 top-4 rounded-sm opacity-70 ring-offset-background transition-opacity hover:opacity-100 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring focus:ring-offset-2 disabled:pointer-events-none data-[state=open]:bg-accent data-[state=open]:text-muted-foreground">
        <X className="h-4 w-4" />
        <span className="sr-only">Close</span>
      </DialogPrimitive.Close>
    </DialogPrimitive.Content>
  </DialogPortal>
))
DialogContent.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Content.displayName

  ...props
}: React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement>) => (

    ref={ref}
    className={cn(
      "fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/80 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
))
DialogOverlay.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Overlay.displayName

const DialogContent = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>
>(({ className, children, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPortal>
    <DialogOverlay />
    <DialogPrimitive.Content
      ref={ref}
      className={cn(
        "fixed left-[50%] top-[50%] z-50 grid w-full max-w-lg translate-x-[-50%] translate-y-[-50%] gap-4 border bg-background p-6 shadow-lg duration-200 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0 data-[state=closed]:zoom-out-95 data-[state=open]:zoom-in-95 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-left-1/2 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-top-[48%] data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-left-1/2 data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-top-[48%] sm:rounded-lg",
        className
      )}
      {...props}
    >
      {children}
      <DialogPrimitive.Close className="absolute right-4 top-4 rounded-sm opacity-70 ring-offset-background transition-opacity hover:opacity-100 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring focus:ring-offset-2 disabled:pointer-events-none data-[state=open]:bg-accent data-[state=open]:text-muted-foreground">
        <X className="h-4 w-4" />
        <span className="sr-only">Close</span>
      </DialogPrimitive.Close>
    </DialogPrimitive.Content>
  </DialogPortal>
))
DialogContent.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Content.displayName

const DialogHeader = ({
  className,
  ...props
}: React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement>) => (
  <div
    className={cn(
      "flex flex-col space-y-1.5 text-center sm:text-left",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
)
DialogHeader.displayName = "DialogHeader"

const DialogFooter = ({
  className,
  ...props

  <div
    className={cn(
      "flex flex-col-reverse sm:flex-row sm:justify-end sm:space-x-2",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
)

>(({ className, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPrimitive.Overlay
    ref={ref}
    className={cn(
      "fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/80 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
))

  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>
>(({ className, children, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPortal>
    <DialogOverlay />
    <DialogPrimitive.Content
      ref={ref}
      className={cn(
        "fixed left-[50%] top-[50%] z-50 grid w-full max-w-lg translate-x-[-50%] translate-y-[-50%] gap-4 border bg-background p-6 shadow-lg duration-200 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0 data-[state=closed]:zoom-out-95 data-[state=open]:zoom-in-95 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-left-1/2 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-top-[48%] data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-left-1/2 data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-top-[48%] sm:rounded-lg",
        className
      )}
      {...props}

    </DialogPrimitive.Content>
  </DialogPortal>
))

  className,
  ...props

  ...props

  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Title>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Title>

      className
    )}

  />
))

DialogTitle.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Title.displayName

const DialogDescription = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Description>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Description>
>(({ className, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPrimitive.Description
    ref={ref}
    className={cn("text-sm text-muted-foreground", className)}
    {...props}
  />
))
DialogDescription.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Description.displayName

  Dialog,
  DialogPortal,
  DialogOverlay,
  DialogClose,
  DialogTrigger,
  DialogContent

import { X } from "lucide-react"

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

const Dialog = DialogPrimitive.Root

  <DialogPrimitive.Overlay
    ref={ref}
    className={cn(
      "fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/80 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
))

  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>

        className
      )}
      {...props}

        <X className="h-4 w-4" />
        <span className="sr-only">Close</span>
      </DialogPrimitive.Close>
    </DialogPrimitive.Content>
  </DialogPortal>
))
DialogContent.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Content.displayName

  className,
  ...props
}: React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement>) => (

    className={cn(

  />

  ...props

    className={cn(

    )}
    {...props}

      "text-lg font-semibold leading-none tracking-tight",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
))
DialogTitle.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Title.displayName

const DialogDescription = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Description>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Description>
>(({ className, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPrimitive.Description
    ref={ref}
    className={cn("text-sm text-muted-foreground", className)}
    {...props}
  />
))
DialogDescription.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Description.displayName

export {
  Dialog,
  DialogPortal,
  DialogOverlay,
  DialogClose,
  DialogTrigger,
  DialogContent,
  DialogHeader,
  DialogFooter,
  DialogTitle,
  DialogDescription

* as React from "react"
import * as DialogPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-dialog"
import { X } from "lucide-react"

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

const Dialog = DialogPrimitive.Root

const DialogTrigger = DialogPrimitive.Trigger

const DialogPortal = DialogPrimitive.Portal

const DialogClose = DialogPrimitive.Close

const DialogOverlay = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>
>(({ className, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPrimitive.Overlay
    ref={ref}
    className={cn(
      "fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/80 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
))
DialogOverlay.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Overlay.displayName

const DialogContent = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content>
>(({ className, children, ...props }, ref) => (
  <DialogPortal>
    <DialogOverlay />
    <DialogPrimitive.Content
      ref={ref}
      className={cn(
        "fixed left-[50%] top-[50%] z-50 grid w-full max-w-lg translate-x-[-50%] translate-y-[-50%] gap-4 border bg-background p-6 shadow-lg duration-200 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0 data-[state=closed]:zoom-out-95 data-[state=open]:zoom-in-95 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-left-1/2 data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-top-[48%] data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-left-1/2 data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-top-[48%] sm:rounded-lg",
        className
      )}
      {...props}
    >
      {children}
      <DialogPrimitive.Close className="absolute right-4 top-4 rounded-sm opacity-70 ring-offset-background transition-opacity hover:opacity-100 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring focus:ring-offset-2 disabled:pointer-events-none data-[state=open]:bg-accent data-[state=open]:text-muted-foreground">
        <X className="h-4 w-4" />
        <span className="sr-only">Close</span>
      </DialogPrimitive.Close>
    </DialogPrimitive.Content>
  </DialogPortal>
))
DialogContent.displayName = DialogPrimitive.Content.displayName

const DialogHeader = ({
  className,
  ...props
}: React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement>) => (
  <div
    className={cn(
      "flex flex-col space-y-1.5 text-center sm:text-left",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
)
DialogHeader.displayName = "DialogHeader"

  className,
  ...props
}: React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement>) => (

    className={cn(
      "flex flex-col-reverse sm:flex-row sm:justify-end sm:space-x-2",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
